                        <span style="padding-left: 5px;">
                            <strong style="font-size:15pt;">Ervin Santana</strong></span>

                    <tr style="background-color: #FFF;"><td style="border-top:2px solid #D3D3D3; font-size:10pt;"><div style="padding-top:5px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px;"><b><a href="http://www.rotowire.com/users/ad_jump.asp?id=688&playerid=6542" style="text-decoration:none;">RotoWire News</a>:</b> Santana gave up five runs over 3.1 innings with three strikeouts, but seven hits including two home runs in Friday's loss to Detroit.                 <tr style="background-color: #FFF;"><td style="border-top:2px solid #D3D3D3; vertical-align:top; padding-bottom:4px; padding-left:5px;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:13pt"><span class="m_date">6/14/2017</span> - <a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/the-sleeper-and-the-bust-episode-453-fast-start-sps/">The Sleeper and the Bust Episode: 453 – Fast Start&raquo;</a><span class="m_comments"> by </span><span class="m_author"><a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/index.php?author=11752">Paul Sporer (RotoGraphs)</a></span><span class="m_comments">&nbsp;<a href="http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/the-sleeper-and-the-bust-episode-453-fast-start-sps/#comments"><img src="images/commentslink.gif" border="0px" />8</a></span><br /></div></td></tr>

                <tr id="so1" style="background-color: #FFF;"><td colspan="5" style="border-top:2px solid #D3D3D3; padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="width:100%; font-size:10pt"><center>Profiles:&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa2" href="javascript:showMoreSO();">2010</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa3" href="javascript:showMoreSO2011();">2011</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa4" href="javascript:showMoreSO2012();">2012</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa5" href="javascript:showMoreSO2013();">2013</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa6" href="javascript:showMoreSO2014();">2014</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa7" href="javascript:showMoreSO2015();">2015</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa8" href="javascript:showMoreSO2016();">2016</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa9"  href="javascript:showMoreSO2017();">2017</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;(Click Year to Expand / <a href="javascript:hideSO('so1');">Close</a>)</center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so2" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Year in Review: </b>Santana opened the year on the disabled list with a sore elbow and did not make his debut until mid-May.  After six starts and a 7.47 ERA, Santana went back on the DL, this time with forearm tightness.  After being sidelined for a month, it took Santana another five weeks, during which batters posted a .904 OPS against him, to work back into shape.  But in his final 11 games of the season, Santana went 4-2 with a 2.84 ERA.  One thing that helped down the stretch was increased velocity on his fastball.  After overpowering hitters in 2008, Santana’s average velocity dropped 2.1 mph, down to 92.3.  But in September, he averaged 93.3 mph with his fastball.  But even with the extra velocity, Santana still struggled with the gopher ball.  He gave up eight homers in 42.2 innings pitched in the final month and finished the year with a 12.8% HR/FB rate, the highest of his career.<br /><br /><b>The Year Ahead: </b>Santana’s batted-ball profile was almost identical between 2008 and 2009.  The difference was that batters teed off on his fastball.  Essentially a neutral pitch in 2008, Santana’s fastball for the year had a -1.39 wFB/C, which would have been the worst mark in the Majors if he had enough innings to qualify.  But in September, with the extra velocity, it had a wFB/C of -0.16, a drastic improvement that bodes well for 2010.  Santana’s slider remained an effective pitch last year.  If he can move closer to 2008-type velocity, Santana should improve on last year’s .320 BABIP (career average: .303), 6.89 K/9 (career average: 7.31), and 12.8% HR/FB mark (career average: 9.9) to once again rank as one of the top pitchers in the American League. (Brian Joura)</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so3" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>For the past six seasons, Ervin Santana has alternated high-inning totals (204, 219, 223) with only medium-inning totals (134, 150, 140). If we judged solely on that pattern, Santana would be due one of those disappointing seasons. Luckily, that is not how we predict usage patterns. However, there are some troubling signs in Santana’s numbers. His strikeout rate dropped again in 2010 and is now below average and the home runs-allowed rose to a career-high 27. Santana is a bit above average at limiting walks, but his WHIP has alternated between above and below average just like his innings total has and is more troubling than the innings pitched. Santana’s 17 wins in 2010 make him a high-profile starting pitcher, but his numbers do not back those up and he’s roughly an average pitcher across the board. How you feel about the Angels chances to crack 85 wins as a team and contend for the playoffs in 2011 will affect your evaluation of Santana, but he will probably be overvalued at the start. (Matthew Carruth)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Ervin Santana needed the Angels to get better this winter to afford him a chance to repeat his 17 wins. They did not and he should not either.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so4" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Thanks to his stretch from 2005 to 2010, you likely view Santana as fragile and flaky. Well, Santana’s performance seems to have flattened out and found its' mark, and the right-hander just posted his second consecutive 200+ inning season, his third in four years. Santana’s strikeout rate sits in the high-sixes and low-sevens while his walk rate tends to stay around three per nine. Santana added grounders to his arsenal in 2011, which was a nice treat for fantasy owners. Santana may get to face off against lesser fourth starters a little more often now that the Halos have brought C.J. Wilson into the fold, so you can expect around 13 or 14 wins in 2012, assuming Santana gets a full season on the mound. (Zach Sanders)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Santana should win 13 or 14 games while posting an ERA in the mid-to-high-threes. He’s not a fantasy stud, but he’s worthy of a pick late in standard-league drafts.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so5" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Following two above-average fantasy seasons, Ervin Santana saw his stock plummet during the 2012 season. Santana’s ERA rose from 3.38 to 5.16 despite a .241 batting average on balls in play, which is the sort of thing that happens when you allow two homers every nine innings. While Santana wasn’t playing in a hitter’s park in L.A., Kansas City will be friendlier for the right-hander, especially when left-handed hitters step up to the plate -- and the righty fastball/slider pitcher does have some troubles against lefties from time to time. KC won’t turn Santana back into the ace he was in 2008, but it should help him get some of his mojo back. If Santana’s ERA is above his 4.33 career mark in 2013, this author will be surprised. (Zach Sanders)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Ervin Santana sucked in 2012, but he’ll be better off in 2013. Take him in the later rounds of deep or AL-only drafts.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so6" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Ervin Santana had a disastrous 2012 season which was mainly caused by his league-leading two homers per nine innings and 18.9% home run per fly ball rate (among qualified starters). Both values were easily career highs. A drop in velocity (92.8 mph to 91.7 mph) and the inability to get left-handed hitters out due to a lack of a change-up (.371 weighted on base average vs. lefties and .288 vs. righties) were the main causes for the decline. The Royals took a chance on Santana in 2013 and it paid off.  As should be expected, his home run values regressed toward his career values. Additionally, after a rocky start, he was able to increase his velocity to his 2011 levels around 92.5 mph. Finally in 2013, he posted a five-year-low walk rate but the cause isn't obvious. He was in the zone a bit more (PITCHf/x zone percentage only). He got hitters to chase a bit more outside. Both don't seem to be major changes. Maybe the Royals' catchers framed pitches better? I expect his future walk rate to be closer to his career value of 2.8. With an expected strikeout rate around seven per nine, those sorts of rates should usually lead to an ERA around 4.20. His value could increase or decrease depending on his next team. If he goes to a large park in the National League with a good defense, he will likely produce decently, but the risk is obvious in a different situation. Some baseline value is there, but until he signs with a team, his true value will be unknown. (Jeff Zimmerman)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Ervin Santana rebounded in 2013 from a disappointing 2012 season by mainly keeping the ball in the park more often. So, much of his 2014 value will be determined by which team ends up signing him, and what park he calls home.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so7" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Ervin Santana pitched better than the 3.95 ERA he recorded last season, but there are some concerns with what to expect out of him as he moves back to the American League this season. Santana saw his strikeouts increase at almost the identical rate that is expected when a player moves from the American League to the National League, so it is reasonable to expect his strikeouts to drop back down around to the 18% mark at which he sat before moving to the Braves. Along with moving back into the tougher league, the Twins have a lackluster defense, highlighted by the acquisition of Torii Hunter in right field. Santana pretty much is who he is at this point, which is roughly a league average pitcher. The only reason he did not throw over 200 innings last year was because he signed late after declining his qualifying offer. While all pitchers are health risks, he has shown some consistency in starting over 30 games in each of the past five seasons. Three of his past four years he has posted between an ERA between 3.24 to 3.95. Despite the health and reliability, the move to the American League is not quite a welcome one, and Santana should only really be looked at as rotational depth in most fantasy formats. Even if the change got better. (Ben Duronio)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Santana had a decent 2014 in the National League, but his move to the American League should lead to a lower strikeout rate. Combine that with a poor defense behind him, and you get a pitcher that will likely be a bit overvalued on draft day despite recording 14 wins last season.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so8" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Santana's Twins career started with disappointment, as a Friday news dump before the season opened reported the right-hander had tested positive for Stanozolol. The suspension which followed cost Santana the first 80 games of his Twins career, and when he returned in July the results were uneven. Month by month, Santana had ERAs of 3.78, 7.11 and 1.88, as he was electric down the stretch for a Twins club attempting to sneak into the postseason. Santana's last seven starts all went at least seven innings, and he had a 1.62 ERA and 47 strikeouts over those 50 innings. Those are the kinds of stretches the Twins need, as they have a rotation that is mostly mid-rotation types with little ace potential. To be clear, there are no expectations for Santana to pitch like an ace, but rather be an anchor for a developing staff. The potential for that sort of work in 2016 seems to be there, especially if he can stay healthy. (Brandon Warne)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Santana will be an interesting back end flier type in fantasy leagues. He was fantastic after a dead arm period in an odd 2015, and might be the Twins' Opening Day starter in 2016.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so9" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Santana was easily the biggest (if not only) bright spot in a Twins rotation that finished last or nearly last in virtually every meaningful statistic. No team had a worse rotation ERA than the Twins, but don't blame Santana, who picked up steam as the season wore on, finishing with a 3.38 ERA — his lowest since 2013 — and good-but-not-great rate stats. It didn't start that way, however, as Santana carried a 5.00-plus ERA well into June. He finished his June 14 start with a 5.10 ERA, but from that point on was absolutely fantastic in his final 18 starts: 2.41 ERA, .589 on-base plus slugging against and a 100-32 strikeout-to-walk ratio in 116 innings. Only once in Santana's final 18 starts did he allow more than three earned runs, and as a result, there was little reason why he was considered one of the Twins' best trading chips, not only at both trading deadlines but also this offseason. As of now, however, it looks as though he'll be with the Twins to start 2017. For a guy who has thrown more than 2,000 innings and fired a lot of sliders, the end is always one sore arm away, but he's been incredibly durable to this point in his career. He threw harder than he had at any point in the last five years in 2016 (92.7 mph average) and thus seems to be a good bet to again be a fairly solid back-end fantasy pitcher. (@Brandon_Warne)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>He's not sexy, but you can do far, far worse for a back-end starter in fantasy leagues. He'll be much more useful in deep leagues, however.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
            </table>
        </td>
        <td style="width: 302px; height: 250px; vertical-align: top;">

    function setAverage(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_average') {


                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'block') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'block'; }
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'table-row') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'table-row'; }
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function setPost(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_postseason' || node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_postseason_total') {


                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'block') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'block'; }
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'table-row') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'table-row'; }
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function setProj(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_projections_show') {

                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function setRegular(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow' || node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgAltRow' || node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_total') {

                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function setProjShow(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_projections_hide') {

                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'block') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'block'; }
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'table-row') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'table-row'; }
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function setMinor(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_minors_show') {

                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == 'none') {
                                vis.display = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                vis.display = 'none';
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    function doNothing() { }

    function setPart(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_multi' || node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_multi') {


                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'block') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'block'; }
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'table-row') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'table-row'; }
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // Create the tooltips only on document load
    $(document).ready(function () {
        // Make sure to only match links to wikipedia with a rel tag
        $('a[tipgloss]').each(function () {
            // We make use of the .each() loop to gain access to each element via the "this" keyword...
            $(this).qtip(
		{
		    content: {
		        // Set the text to an image HTML string with the correct src URL to the loading image you want to use
		        text: " ",
		        ajax: {
		            url: $(this).attr('tipgloss') // Use the rel attribute of each element for the url to load
		        }
		    },
		    position: {
		        viewport: $(window),
		        at: "top center",
		        my: "bottom center",
		        effect: false
		    },
		    show: {
		        event: "click mouseenter",
		        solo: true // Only show one tooltip at a time
		    },
		    hide: {
		        event: "click mouseleave",
		        delay: 1000,
		        fixed: true
		    },
		    style: {
		        classes: "qtip-light"
		    }
		})

            // Make sure it doesn't follow the link when we click it
        });
    });
